To implement the requested Python program for a custom computer-vision model, we will structure our application into several core components. Below is a high-level overview of the architecture, including the names of the core classes, functions, and methods, along with their purposes.

### Core Components

1. **main.py**: The entry point of the application that initializes the GUI and handles user interactions.
2. **model.py**: Contains the definition of the computer vision model using TensorFlow/PyTorch.
3. **data_loader.py**: Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
4. **train.py**: Handles the training process of the model.
5. **api.py**: Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
6. **gui.py**: Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
7. **utils.py**: Utility functions for various tasks (e.g., saving/loading models, logging).

### Implementation

Let's start with the `main.py` file.

#### main.py

```python
'''
Main entry point of the application that initializes the GUI and handles user interactions.
'''

import tkinter as tk
from gui import Application

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = Application(master=root)
    app.mainloop()
```

#### model.py

```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''

import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

#### data_loader.py

```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''

import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

#### train.py

```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''

from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader

class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()

    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

#### api.py

```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

#### gui.py

```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog
from train import Trainer

class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()

        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()

    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        tk.messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")

```

#### utils.py

```python
'''
Utility functions for various tasks (e.g., saving/loading models, logging).
'''

import logging

def setup_logging():
    logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')

def log_message(message):
    logging.info(message)
```

### Summary

This implementation provides a complete structure for a custom computer-vision model using TensorFlow, including a GUI for user interaction, data loading, model training, and a REST API for inference. Each file is modular, allowing for easy maintenance and updates. The GUI allows users to select a directory for training data and initiate the training process. 

Make sure to install the necessary libraries (TensorFlow, Flask, OpenCV, etc.) before running the application.

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program for a custom computer-vision model that learns visual patterns from still images efficiently, utilizing TensorFlow/PyTorch for end-to-end development, including training, packaging for deployment behind a REST/gRPC interface, and providing thorough documentation and code reproducibility.".

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        tk.messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        tk.messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

**main.py**
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

**data_loader.py**
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program for a custom computer-vision model that learns visual patterns from still images efficiently, utilizing TensorFlow/PyTorch for end-to-end development, including training, packaging for deployment behind a REST/gRPC interface, and providing thorough documentation and code reproducibility.".

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

       return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
   ```

2. **In `train.py`**, add validation for the training data:
   ```python
   def train_model(self, epochs=10):
       train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
       if len(train_data) == 0 or len(train_labels) == 0:
           raise ValueError("No training data found. Please check the data directory.")
       self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
       self.model.save_model('model.h5')
   ```

3. **In `gui.py`**, handle cases where the user cancels the directory selection:
   ```python
   def train_model(self):
       data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
       if not data_directory:  # User canceled the dialog
           messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "No directory selected.")
           return
       trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
       trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
       messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
   ```

Implementing these changes will enhance the robustness of the application and improve user experience by preventing unexpected crashes and providing clear feedback.

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program for a custom computer-vision model that learns visual patterns from still images efficiently, utilizing TensorFlow/PyTorch for end-to-end development, including training, packaging for deployment behind a REST/gRPC interface, and providing thorough documentation and code reproducibility.".

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")

```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

**data_loader.py**
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):

        self.model = CustomModel()

**main.py**
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

**data_loader.py**
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

**train.py**
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader

class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()

    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for various tasks (e.g., saving/loading models, logging).

import logging
def setup_logging():
    logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
def log_message(message):
    logging.info(message)

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    data = request.json
    image = np.array(data['image'])  # Expecting a list of pixel values
    image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
    prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
    return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

**main.py**
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

**data_loader.py**
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

**main.py**
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

**model.py**
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

**data_loader.py**
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
try:
    import tensorflow as tf
    from model import CustomModel
except ImportError as e:
    raise ImportError("TensorFlow is not installed. Please install TensorFlow to run this application.") from e

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging

app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')

@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

FILENAME
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
try:
    import tensorflow as tf
    from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
except ImportError as e:
    raise ImportError("TensorFlow is not installed. Please install TensorFlow to run this application.") from e

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

FILENAME
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

try:
    import tensorflow as tf
    from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
except ImportError as e:
    raise ImportError("TensorFlow is not installed. Please install TensorFlow to run this application.") from e

class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()

    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model

    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)

    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)

    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

FILENAME
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array

class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory

    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

FILENAME
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader

class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()

    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer

class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()

    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

train.py
```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.
'''
from model import CustomModel
from data_loader import DataLoader
class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')
```

gui.py
```python
'''
Contains the GUI implementation using Tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import filedialog, messagebox
from train import Trainer
class Application(tk.Frame):
    def __init__(self, master=None):
        super().__init__(master)
        self.master = master
        self.pack()
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        self.train_button = tk.Button(self)
        self.train_button["text"] = "Train Model"
        self.train_button["command"] = self.train_model
        self.train_button.pack()
        self.quit = tk.Button(self, text="QUIT", fg="red",
                              command=self.master.destroy)
        self.quit.pack()
    def train_model(self):
        data_directory = filedialog.askdirectory()
        trainer = Trainer(data_directory)
        trainer.train_model(epochs=10)
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "Training Complete!")
```

    logging.info(message)

```main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

```model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

```data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

 ```main.py
```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

```model.py
```python
'''
Defines the custom computer vision model using TensorFlow.
'''
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras import layers, models
class CustomModel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_model()
    def build_model(self):
        model = models.Sequential([
            layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), activation='relu', input_shape=(128, 128, 3)),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), activation='relu'),
            layers.MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(2, 2)),
            layers.Flatten(),
            layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            layers.Dense(10, activation='softmax')  # Assuming 10 classes
        ])
        model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', metrics=['accuracy'])
        return model
    def train(self, train_data, train_labels, epochs=10):
        self.model.fit(train_data, train_labels, epochs=epochs)
    def save_model(self, filepath):
        self.model.save(filepath)
    def load_model(self, filepath):
        self.model = models.load_model(filepath)
```

```data_loader.py
```python
'''
Responsible for loading and preprocessing the image data.
'''
import os
import numpy as np
from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
class DataLoader:
    def __init__(self, directory):
        self.directory = directory
    def load_data(self):
        images = []
        labels = []
        for label in os.listdir(self.directory):
            label_dir = os.path.join(self.directory, label)
            if os.path.isdir(label_dir):
                for img_file in os.listdir(label_dir):
                    img_path = os.path.join(label_dir, img_file)
                    img = load_img(img_path, target_size=(128, 128))
                    img_array = img_to_array(img) / 255.0  # Normalize
                    images.append(img_array)
                    labels.append(int(label))  # Assuming labels are integers
        return np.array(images), np.array(labels)
```

```python
'''
Handles the training process of the model.

class Trainer:
    def __init__(self, data_directory):
        self.data_loader = DataLoader(data_directory)
        self.model = CustomModel()
    def train_model(self, epochs=10):
        train_data, train_labels = self.data_loader.load_data()
        self.model.train(train_data, train_labels, epochs)
        self.model.save_model('model.h5')

```python
'''
Implements the REST/gRPC interface for model inference.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
from model import CustomModel
import numpy as np
import cv2
import logging
app = Flask(__name__)
model = CustomModel()
model.load_model('model.h5')
@app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
def predict():
    try:
        data = request.json
        if 'image' not in data:
            return jsonify({'error': 'No image provided'}), 400
        image = np.array(data['image'])
        # Check if the image has the correct shape
        if image.shape != (128, 128, 3):
            return jsonify({'error': 'Image must be of shape (128, 128, 3)'}), 400
        image = cv2.resize(image, (128, 128)) / 255.0  # Resize and normalize
        prediction = model.model.predict(np.expand_dims(image, axis=0))
        return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
